### Dirty War ###

MEX_setup_DW_connections = {
	# Setup connections to render
	clear_array = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_start
	clear_array = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_end

	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_locations
		value = first_loc

		for_each_loop = {
			array = first_loc:MEX_DW_connections
			value = second_loc


			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { first_loc < second_loc } }
				log = "[?first_loc] [?second_loc]"

				add_to_array = { MEX_DW_rendered_connections_start = first_loc }
				add_to_array = { MEX_DW_rendered_connections_end = second_loc }
			}
		}
	}

	clear_array = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_diff_x
	clear_array = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_diff_y
	clear_array = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_frame
	clear_array = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_f2s

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_start^num
		value = i

		set_temp_variable = { first_loc = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_start^i }
		set_temp_variable = { second_loc = MEX_DW_rendered_connections_end^i }

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { first_loc:MEX_DW_x > second_loc:MEX_DW_x } }
			set_temp_variable = { connection_x = second_loc:MEX_DW_x }
			set_temp_variable = { difference_x = first_loc:MEX_DW_x }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { difference_x = second_loc:MEX_DW_x }

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { first_loc:MEX_DW_y > second_loc:MEX_DW_y } }
				set_temp_variable = { connection_y = second_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { difference_y = first_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { difference_y = second_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { toggle = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { f2s = 0 }
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { connection_y = first_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { difference_y = second_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { difference_y = first_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { toggle = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { f2s = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { connection_x = first_loc:MEX_DW_x }
			set_temp_variable = { difference_x = second_loc:MEX_DW_x }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { difference_x = first_loc:MEX_DW_x }

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { first_loc:MEX_DW_y > second_loc:MEX_DW_y } }
				set_temp_variable = { connection_y = second_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { difference_y = first_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { difference_y = second_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { toggle = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { f2s = 0 }
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { connection_y = first_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { difference_y = second_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { difference_y = first_loc:MEX_DW_y }
				set_temp_variable = { toggle = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { f2s = 1 }
			}
		}



		divide_temp_variable = { difference_x = 10 }
		divide_temp_variable = { difference_y = 10 }

		round_temp_variable = difference_x
		round_temp_variable = difference_y



		set_temp_variable = { connection_frame = toggle }
		multiply_temp_variable = { connection_frame = 1000 }
		round_temp_variable = connection_frame
		add_to_temp_variable = { connection_frame = difference_x }
		multiply_temp_variable = { connection_frame = 1000 }
		round_temp_variable = connection_frame
		add_to_temp_variable = { connection_frame = difference_y }

		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_rendered_connections_diff_x = connection_x }
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_rendered_connections_diff_y = connection_y }
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_rendered_connections_frame = connection_frame }
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_rendered_connections_f2s = f2s }
	}
}

MEX_DW_setup_node = {
	clear_array = MEX_DW_influence
	clear_array = MEX_DW_connections

	set_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = MEX.TOWN }
	set_variable = { MEX_DW_x = 0 }
	set_variable = { MEX_DW_y = 0 }

	set_variable = { MEX_DW_supply = 10 }
	set_variable = { MEX_DW_supply_storage = 0 }


	set_variable = { MEX_DW_intel = 0 }
	#set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT }
}

MEX_DW_clear_all_top_arrs = {
	clear_array = MEX_DW_gen_info_box
	clear_array = MEX_DW_recruit_unit_box
	clear_array = MEX_DW_node_info_box
	clear_array = MEX_DW_more_info_box
}
d_action_log = {
	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_times   index = 0 value = GLOBAL.date }
	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_actors  index = 0 value = args^4 }
	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_types   index = 0 value = 0 }
	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_targets index = 0 value = MEX.MEX_DW_locations^1 }
}

d_dw_owner = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { MEX_DW_selected_location > 0 } }

		var:MEX_DW_selected_location = {
			set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = args^0 }
		}
	}
}

	d_faction = yes
}

}

	d_faction = yes
}
#args^0 = node, args^1 = faction
d_faction = {
	set_temp_variable = { can_we_create_log_entry = 0 }
	var:args^0 = {
		set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = var:args^1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				MEX_dw_is_node_allegence_known = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { can_we_create_log_entry = 1 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { can_we_create_log_entry = 1 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { value_of_event_type = token:MEX_DW_Event_Enemy_Takes_Node }
		MEX_DW_create_event_log_entry = yes
	}
	MEX_get_controlled_nodes = yes #regenerate stronghold controls
}

MEX_DW_create_event_log_entry = {
	set_temp_variable = { new_event_entry = EVENT_HOLDER }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			MEX_DW_setup_event_type_[VALUE_OF_EVENT] = yes
		}
		VALUE_OF_EVENT = "[?value_of_event_type.GetTokenKey]"
	}
	set_variable = { event_type@var:new_event_entry = value_of_event_type }

	add_to_array = {
		array = MEX_DW_events
		value = new_event_entry
		index = 0
	}

	MEX_DW_filter_actions_or_events = yes
	add_to_variable = { EVENT_HOLDER = 1 }
}

MEX_DW_setup_event_type_MEX_DW_Event_Enemy_Takes_Node = {
	set_variable = { node_value_to_take@var:new_event_entry = args^0 }
	set_variable = { node_faction_taking@var:new_event_entry = args^1 }

}

d_town = {
	var:args^0 = {
		set_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = MEX.TOWN }
	}
}

d_stronghold = {
	set_variable = { MEX_main_stronghold = 0 }
	set_variable = { MEX_main_stronghold = args^0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { MEX_main_stronghold = 0 }
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_all_strongholds = MEX_main_stronghold }
	}

	var:args^0 = {
		set_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = MEX.STRONGHOLD }
		set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = token:MEX_Faction_THE_GPG }
		set_variable = { MEX_DW_organization = 50 }
		set_variable = { MEX_DW_supply = 0 }
	}
	MEX_get_controlled_nodes = yes
}

mex_testfff = {
	set_temp_variable = { args^0 = MEX_DW_selected_location }
	set_temp_variable = { args^1 = token:MEX_Faction_LOS_TECOS }
	set_temp_variable = { args^2 = token:MEX_UNIT_AIR_STRIKE }
	set_temp_variable = { args^3 = 300 }
	set_temp_variable = { args^4 = base_node_dist@token:MEX_UNIT_AIR_STRIKE }
	d_units = yes
}
#use to spawn units, args^0 is node, args^1 is alliegance, args^2 is Unit type,args^3 is number of units, args^4 is nodes travelable check mex_testfff for more info
d_units = {

	var:args^0 = {
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_node_units = MEX.UNIT_HOLDER }
	}
	#ALL NEEDED
	add_to_variable = { UNIT_HOLDER:MEX_DW_node_num_units = args^3 }
	set_variable = { UNIT_HOLDER:MEX_DW_alliegance = args^1}
	set_variable = { UNIT_HOLDER:MEX_DW_NODES_TRAVELABLE = args^4 }
	set_variable = { UNIT_HOLDER:MEX_DW_UNIT_TYPE = args^2 }
	#log = [?UNIT_HOLDER:MEX_DW_node_num_units]
	add_to_variable = { UNIT_HOLDER = 1}

}

MEX_mover_helper_func = {
	set_temp_variable = { node_From = 12 }
	set_temp_variable = { node_To = 19 }
	var:node_From = {
		add_to_temp_array = { selected_regiments = MEX_DW_node_units^0 }
	}
	MEX_DW_move_regiment = yes
}

MEX_DW_move_regiment = {
	# node_From, node_To, selected_regiments - make sure this array doesnt have units have you arent supposed to move!,
	log = [?selected_regiments^0]

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { selected_regiments^num > 0 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { node_A = node_From }
		set_temp_variable = { node_B = node_To }
		MEX_dw_node_traversal = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = selected_regiments
			value = regiment



			set_temp_variable = { maxnodes = regiment:MEX_DW_NODES_TRAVELABLE }
			add_to_temp_variable = { maxnodes = 1}

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = { #yes im lazy
						check_variable = { maxnodes > path^num }
						check_variable = { maxnodes = path^num }
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { regiment:MEX_DW_NODES_TRAVELABLE = path^num }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { regiment:MEX_DW_NODES_TRAVELABLE < 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { regiment:MEX_DW_NODES_TRAVELABLE = 0 }
				}
				var:node_To = {
					add_to_array = { MEX_DW_node_units = regiment }
				}
				var:node_From = {
					remove_from_array = { array = MEX_DW_node_units			value = regiment }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

MEX_get_controlled_nodes = {
	#set_temp_variable = { loc_index = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_locations
		value = loc

		clear_array = loc:MEX_DW_distance
		clear_array = loc:MEX_DW_supply_through

		set_temp_variable = { mex_dist_index = 0 }
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = { check_variable = { mex_dist_index < MEX_DW_all_strongholds^num } }

			set_variable = { loc:MEX_DW_distance^mex_dist_index = -1 }
			set_variable = { loc:MEX_DW_supply_through^mex_dist_index = 0 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { mex_dist_index = 1 }
		}

		#set_variable = { loc:MEX_DW_distance^0 = -1 }

	}
	set_temp_variable = { new_stronghold_index = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_all_strongholds
		value = stronghold

		set_temp_variable = { group = stronghold:MEX_DW_controller }

		clear_temp_array = to_explore
		clear_array = stronghold:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes
		clear_array = stronghold:MEX_DW_connected_nodes


		add_to_temp_array = { to_explore = stronghold }
		set_variable = { stronghold:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_nodes_explored = 0 }
		add_to_array = { stronghold:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes = stronghold }

		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { MEX_DW_nodes_explored < 7 }
					check_variable = { to_explore^num > 0 }
				}
			}

			set_temp_variable = { exploring = to_explore^0 }
			remove_from_temp_array = { array = to_explore index = 0 }

			#add_to_variable = { exploring:MEX_DW_supply_through^new_stronghold_index = exploring:MEX_DW_supply }

			for_each_loop = {
				array = exploring:MEX_DW_connections
				value = exploring_adjacent


				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_controller = group } }

					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = -1 } }

						set_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_parent^new_stronghold_index = exploring }

						set_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = exploring:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index }
						add_to_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 1 }

						add_to_temp_array = { to_explore = exploring_adjacent }
						add_to_array = { stronghold:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes = exploring_adjacent }

					}
				}
				else = {

					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = -1 } }
						set_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = exploring:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index }
						add_to_variable = { exploring_adjacent:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 1 }

						add_to_array = { stronghold:MEX_DW_connected_nodes = exploring_adjacent }

					}

				}
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_nodes_explored = 1 }
		}

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = stronghold:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes^num
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { node_i = stronghold:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes^num }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { node_i = i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { node_i = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { node = stronghold:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes^node_i }

			set_temp_variable = { weighted_dist_supplythru = 0 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { weighted_dist_supplythru = node:MEX_DW_supply }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { node:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 1 }
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { weighted_dist_supplythru = 1.2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { node:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 2 }
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { weighted_dist_supplythru = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { node:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 3 }
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { weighted_dist_supplythru = 0.8 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { node:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 4 }
						check_variable = { node:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 5 }
						check_variable = { node:MEX_DW_distance^new_stronghold_index = 6 }
					}
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { weighted_dist_supplythru = 0.5 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { node:MEX_DW_supply_through^new_stronghold_index = weighted_dist_supplythru }

			set_temp_variable = { parent = node:MEX_DW_parent^new_stronghold_index }


			add_to_variable = { parent:MEX_DW_supply_through^new_stronghold_index = node:MEX_DW_supply_through^new_stronghold_index }
		}
		log = "[?stronghold] [?stronghold:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes^num]"
		add_to_temp_variable = { new_stronghold_index = 1 }
	}
}

MEX_DW_transfer_supplies = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_all_strongholds
		value = stronghold_val

		set_temp_variable = { supply_gen = stronghold_val:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes^num }
		multiply_temp_variable = { supply_gen = 5 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { supply_gen = 15 }

		set_variable = { stronghold_val:MEX_DW_organization = supply_gen }
		clamp_variable = {
			variable = stronghold_val:MEX_DW_organization
			max = 100
			min = 0
		}
		set_temp_variable = { thru_all_nodes = 1 }
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { thru_all_nodes < stronghold_val:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes^num }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { connected_node_sup = stronghold_val:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes^thru_all_nodes }

			set_temp_variable = { Node_A = stronghold_val }
			set_temp_variable = { Node_B = connected_node_sup }
			MEX_dw_node_traversal = yes

			set_temp_variable = { path_dist_mex_dw = path^num }
			clear_array = path
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { path_dist_mex_dw = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { value_of_supply_flow = stronghold_val:MEX_DW_organization }
			divide_temp_variable = { value_of_supply_flow = path_dist_mex_dw }
			set_variable = { connected_node_sup:MEX_DW_supply_through = value_of_supply_flow }

			add_to_temp_variable = { thru_all_nodes = 1 }
		}
	}
}

MEX_DW_set_nodes_supply = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_all_strongholds
		value = stronghold_val

		for_each_loop = {
			array = stronghold_val:MEX_DW_controlled_nodes
			value = strong_controll_node

			add_to_variable = { strong_controll_node:MEX_DW_supply = connected_node_sup:MEX_DW_supply_through }
			clamp_variable = {
				variable = strong_controll_node:MEX_DW_supply
				max = 100
				min = 0
			}

			set_temp_variable = { dec_supply = strong_controll_node:MEX_DW_node_units^num }
			multiply_temp_variable = { dec_supply = 10 }
			subtract_from_variable = { strong_controll_node:MEX_DW_supply = dec_supply }

			clamp_variable = {
				variable = strong_controll_node:MEX_DW_supply
				max = 100
				min = 0
			}
		}

	}
}
MEX_dw_print_nodes = {
	set_temp_variable = { node_number_display = 1 }

	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX.MEX_DW_locations
		value = loc

		var:loc = {
			set_variable = { MEX_DW_print_node_number = node_number_display }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { node_number_display = 1 }
	}

	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX.MEX_DW_locations
		value = loc


		log = "[?loc] = {"
		log = "	set_variable = { MEX_DW_x = [?loc:MEX_DW_x|0] }"
		log = "	set_variable = { MEX_DW_y = [?loc:MEX_DW_y|0] }"
		log = "	set_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = [?loc:MEX_DW_node_type|0] }"
		log = " "
		for_each_loop = {
			array = loc:MEX_DW_connections
			value = second_loc

			log = "	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_connections = [?second_loc] }"
		}
		log = "}"
	}

}

MEX_DW_editor_node_click = {

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 2 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_selected_location = 0 }
		remove_from_array = { array = MEX.MEX_DW_locations value = location_id }

		for_each_loop = {
			array = MEX.MEX_DW_locations
			value = loc

			remove_from_array = { array = loc:MEX_DW_connections value = location_id }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 3 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_last_location = location_id }
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 4 }
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_selected_location = location_id }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 4 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_last_location = location_id } }
		}
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_selected_location = 0 }

		set_temp_variable = { first_node = MEX.MEX_DW_editor_last_location }
		set_temp_variable = { second_node = location_id }
		MEX_dw_add_connection = yes

		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 5 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_last_location = location_id }
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 6 }
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_selected_location = location_id }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 6 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_last_location = location_id } }
		}
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_selected_location = 0 }

		set_temp_variable = { first_node = MEX.MEX_DW_editor_last_location }
		set_temp_variable = { second_node = location_id }
		MEX_dw_remove_connection = yes

		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 7 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_last_location = location_id }
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 8 }
		set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_selected_location = location_id }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 9 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = MEX.GOVERNMENT }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 10 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = MEX.THE_GPG }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 11 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = MEX.TOWN }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 12 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = MEX.CITY }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_editor_mode = 13 }
		}

		set_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = MEX.STRONGHOLD }
	}

	MEX = {
		MEX_setup_DW_connections = yes
	}
}

	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_actors  index = 0 value = GOVERNMENT }
	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_types   index = 0 value = 0 }
	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_targets index = 0 value = MEX.MEX_DW_locations^108 }
}

	add_to_array = { array = MEX_DW_action_log_actors  index = 0 value = THE_GPG }

}

	set_temp_variable = { holdd = nodesel:MEX_DW_node_units^0}

	log = [?holdd:MEX_DW_NODES_TRAVELABLE]
}

	log = "[?GLOBAL.date.GetDateStringNoHourLong] [?display_date]"
	log = "[MEX_DW_days_ago]"

	set_temp_variable = { action_idx = 0 }
	log = "[MEX_DW_action_desc]"
}




MEX_close_dw_map_editor = {
	clr_country_flag = MEX_DW_editor_active
	set_variable = { MEX_DW_editor_mode = 0 }
	clear_array = MEX_DW_editor_tile_x
	clear_array = MEX_DW_editor_tile_y
}

MEX_setup_new_dw_map_editor = {

	set_country_flag = MEX_DW_editor_active

	clear_array = MEX_DW_editor_tile_x
	clear_array = MEX_DW_editor_tile_y

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 125
		value = x

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 75
			value = y

			set_temp_variable = { x_pos = x }
			multiply_temp_variable = { x_pos = 50 }
			set_temp_variable = { y_pos = y }
			multiply_temp_variable = { y_pos = 50 }
			add_to_array = { MEX_DW_editor_tile_x = x_pos }
			add_to_array = { MEX_DW_editor_tile_y = y_pos }

		}
	}
}

MEX_dw_add_connection = {
	MEX_dw_remove_connection = yes

	var:first_node = {
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_connections = second_node }
	}
	var:second_node = {
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_connections = first_node }
	}
}

MEX_dw_remove_connection = {

	var:first_node = {
		remove_from_array = { array = MEX_DW_connections value = second_node }
	}
	var:second_node = {
		remove_from_array = { array = MEX_DW_connections value = first_node }
	}
}


MEX_dw_place_new_node = {
	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_locations = MEX_DW_next_location_id }

	var:MEX_DW_next_location_id = {
		MEX_DW_setup_node = yes

		set_variable = { MEX_DW_x = new_node_x }
		set_variable = { MEX_DW_y = new_node_y }
	}

	add_to_variable = { MEX_DW_next_location_id = 1 }

	MEX_setup_DW_connections = yes
}

MEX_DW_DFS_generate_intel = {
	clear_temp_array = visited

	set_temp_variable = { node:depth = 0 }
	add_to_temp_array = { queue = node }
	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { queue^num > 0 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { last = queue^num }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { last = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { newnode = queue^last }
		remove_from_temp_array = { queue = newnode }
		set_temp_variable = { depth = newnode:depth }

		set_temp_variable = { depthmodifier = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { depth = 0 }
				}
			}
			divide_temp_variable = { depthmodifier = depth }
		}


		multiply_temp_variable = { depthmodifier = MEX.DFS_AGENTS_INTEL_GEN }


		set_temp_variable = { amount = dfs_total }
		multiply_temp_variable = { amount = depthmodifier }

		add_to_variable = { newnode:MEX_DW_intel = amount }


		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { depth < 7 }
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = newnode:MEX_DW_connections
				value = neighbour
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_in_array = {
								array = visited
								value = neighbour
							}
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { tempdepth = 0 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { tempdepth = depth }

					add_to_temp_variable = { tempdepth = 1 }
					log = [?depth]
					log = [?tempdepth]
					set_temp_variable = { neighbour:depth = tempdepth }



					add_to_temp_array = { queue = neighbour }
					add_to_temp_array = { visited = neighbour }

				}
			}
		}

	}
}

MEX_DW_turn_tick = {
	#intel
	MEX_DW_turn_tick_intel = yes

	#enemy supply
	MEX_DW_transfer_supplies = yes
	MEX_DW_set_nodes_supply = yes
}
MEX_DW_turn_tick_intel = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_locations
		value = node_location


		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { node_location:MEX_DW_node_units^num > 0 }
				check_variable = { node_location:MEX_DW_intel < 100 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { new_intel_value = node_location:MEX_DW_intel }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = node_location:MEX_DW_node_units
				value = loc_unit_value


				set_temp_variable = { temp_intel_value = new_intel_value }

				set_temp_variable = { unit_type_value = loc_unit_value:MEX_DW_UNIT_TYPE }
				set_temp_variable = { unit_init_intel_value = base_intel_gen@var:unit_type_value }
				multiply_temp_variable = { unit_init_intel_value = loc_unit_value:MEX_DW_node_num_units }
				log = [?unit_init_intel_value]
				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_intel_value = unit_init_intel_value }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { temp_intel_value > 100 } }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { new_intel_value = temp_intel_value }
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { unit_type_value = token:MEX_UNIT_DFS_AGENT }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { dfs_intel_mult = 0.5 }
					for_each_loop = {
						array = node_location:MEX_DW_connections
						value = node_loc_conn

						set_temp_variable = { temp_conn_intel = node_loc_conn:MEX_DW_intel }
						set_temp_variable = { conn_dfs_val = unit_init_intel_value }
						multiply_temp_variable = { conn_dfs_val = dfs_intel_mult }
						add_to_temp_variable = { temp_conn_intel = conn_dfs_val }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { temp_conn_intel < 100 }
							}
							set_variable = { node_loc_conn:MEX_DW_intel = temp_conn_intel }
						}

						for_each_loop = {
							array = node_loc_conn:MEX_DW_connections
							value = node_conn_conn

							set_temp_variable = { temp_conn_2_intel = node_conn_conn:MEX_DW_intel }
							set_temp_variable = { conn_dfs_2_val = conn_dfs_val }
							multiply_temp_variable = { conn_dfs_2_val = dfs_intel_mult }
							add_to_temp_variable = { temp_conn_2_intel = conn_dfs_2_val }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { temp_conn_2_intel < 100 }
								}
								set_variable = { node_conn_conn:MEX_DW_intel = temp_conn_2_intel }
							}
						}

					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { node_location:MEX_DW_intel = new_intel_value }
		}
	}
}

DW_MEX_modify_recruitment_size = {
	#basically, we attempt to add modif_change (-+10,-+50) to the new amount of recruitable units in a regiment, and then do a ton of checks to see if we have enough equipment to handle said units.
	#if this stops working, dont contact shukla. idk what is happening


	set_temp_variable = { newtotal = recruit_amount@var:MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array_value }

	add_to_temp_variable = { newtotal = modif_change }
	clear_array = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names
	clear_array = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_num
	clear_array = MEX_DW_values_to_inc


	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { newtotal > -1 }
		}


		for_each_loop = {
			array = equipment_required_name@var:MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array_value
			value = checkerrrr

			add_to_array = { MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names = checkerrrr }

		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = equipment_required_num@var:MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array_value
			value = checkerrrr


			add_to_array = { MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_num = checkerrrr }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { arr_upper = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { can_continue = 0 }

		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { can_continue = 0 }
				check_variable = { arr_upper < MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names^num }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { equipment_name = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names^arr_upper }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_dw_equipment_num = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_num^arr_upper }
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp_dw_equipment_num = newtotal }
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_temp_variable = { code_name = token:[EQ_DW_NAME]_code_name }
				}
				EQ_DW_NAME = "[?equipment_name.GetTokenKey]"
			}
			set_temp_variable = { sum_temp_dw_equipment_num = temp_dw_equipment_num }

			for_each_loop = {
				array = MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array
				value = units_to_recruit_analysis

				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { recruit_amount@var:units_to_recruit_analysis > 0 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { units_to_recruit_analysis = MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array_value } }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { index_of_eq = 0 }
					for_each_loop = {
						array = equipment_required_name@var:units_to_recruit_analysis
						value = find_the_eq_thingy
						break = break_value_thingy

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { find_the_eq_thingy = equipment_name }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { break_value_thingy = 2 }
						}
						else = {
							add_to_temp_variable = { index_of_eq = 1 }
						}

					}
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							add_to_temp_variable = { sum_temp_dw_equipment_num = MEX_DW_[ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME_THINGY]_unit_calc_val^index_of_eq }
						}
						ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME_THINGY = "[?units_to_recruit_analysis.GetTokenKey]"
					}
				}

			}
			log = "[?equipment_name.GetTokenLocalizedKey]: [?sum_temp_dw_equipment_num]"

			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { sum_temp_dw_equipment_num > num_equipment@[ACTUAL_EQ_NAME]_equipment }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { can_continue = 1 }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_array = { MEX_DW_values_to_inc = temp_dw_equipment_num }

					}
				}
				ACTUAL_EQ_NAME = "[?code_name.GetTokenLocalizedKey]"
			}

			add_to_temp_variable = { arr_upper = 1 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { can_continue = 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { recruit_amount@var:MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array_value = newtotal }
			set_temp_variable = { new_upper = 0 }

			for_each_loop = {
				array = MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array
				value = can_we_actually_recruit_val
				break = we_can_break

				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { recruit_amount@var:can_we_actually_recruit_val > 0}
					}
					set_variable = { MEX_DW_Can_Recruit_Unit = 1 }
					set_temp_variable = { we_can_break = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { MEX_DW_Can_Recruit_Unit = 0 }
				}
			}

			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					clear_array = MEX_DW_[ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME]_unit_calc_val
				}
				ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME = "[?MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array_value.GetTokenKey]"
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { new_upper < MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names^num }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { temp_code_value = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names^new_upper }
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						add_to_array = { MEX_DW_[ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME]_unit_calc_val = MEX_DW_values_to_inc^new_upper }
					}
					ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME = "[?MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array_value.GetTokenKey]"
				}

				add_to_temp_variable = { new_upper = 1 }
			}

		}
	}

	clear_array = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names
	clear_array = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_num
	clear_array = MEX_DW_values_to_inc
}

MEX_DW_Recruit_Unit_Clear_Everything = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array
		value = each_unit_value

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { recruit_amount@var:each_unit_value > 0 }
			}
			#use to spawn units, args^0 is node, args^1 is alliegance, args^2 is Unit type,args^3 is number of units, args^4 is nodes travelable check mex_testfff for more info
			set_temp_variable = { args^0 = MEX_DW_selected_location }
			set_temp_variable = { args^1 = token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT }
			set_temp_variable = { args^2 = each_unit_value }
			set_temp_variable = { args^3 = recruit_amount@var:each_unit_value }
			set_temp_variable = { args^4 = base_node_dist@var:each_unit_value }
			d_units = yes

			for_each_loop = {
				array = equipment_required_name@var:each_unit_value
				value = checkerrrr

				add_to_array = { MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names = checkerrrr }

			}
			set_temp_variable = { incrementer_value_thing = 0 }
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { incrementer_value_thing < MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names^num }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { real_name_value = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names^incrementer_value_thing }
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						set_temp_variable = { code_name_value = token:[ACTUAL_EQ_NAME_VALUE]_code_name }
						set_temp_variable = { values_to_decr = MEX_DW_[ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME]_unit_calc_val^incrementer_value_thing }
						multiply_temp_variable = { values_to_decr = -1 }
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = [CODE_EQ_VALUE]_equipment
							amount = values_to_decr
						}
					}
					ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME = "[?each_unit_value.GetTokenKey]"
					ACTUAL_EQ_NAME_VALUE = "[?real_name_value.GetTokenKey]"
					CODE_EQ_VALUE = "[?code_name_value.GetTokenLocalizedKey]"
				}

				add_to_temp_variable = { incrementer_value_thing = 1 }
			}

			clear_array = MEX_DW_Faction_Req_Eq_token_names
		}
		set_variable = { recruit_amount@var:each_unit_value = 0 }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				clear_array = MEX_DW_[ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME]_unit_calc_val
			}
			ACTUAL_UNIT_NAME = "[?each_unit_value.GetTokenKey]"
		}
	}
	set_variable = { MEX_DW_Can_Recruit_Unit = 0 }
}

MEX_initialize_new_DW = {
	set_variable = { UNIT_HOLDER = 1 }
	set_variable = { EVENT_HOLDER = 1 }
	set_variable = { ACTION_HOLDER = 1}

	set_variable = { TOWN = 0 }
	set_variable = { CITY = 1 }
	set_variable = { STRONGHOLD = 2 }


	set_variable = { BASE_TECH = 1 }

	set_variable = { MEX_DW_Recruit_Click_Change = 20 }
	set_variable = { MEX_DW_Recruit_Shift_Click_Change = 100 }

	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_THE_GPG
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_PDLP
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_FLN
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_ACNR
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_ACG
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_WBoAS
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_MAR
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_UPLAA
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_AGPGP
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_AFNR
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_UNS
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_LOS_TECOS
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_LOS_HALCONES
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_CRWPUP
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_WHITE_GUARDS
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_BLUE_ARMY
	add_ideas = MEX_Faction_TBDSYN


	add_ideas = MEX_UNIT_SOLDIER
	add_ideas = MEX_UNIT_DFS_AGENT
	add_ideas = MEX_UNIT_FJP
	add_ideas = MEX_UNIT_AIR_STRIKE
	add_ideas = MEX_UNIT_ORD_SPECIAL_FORCE
	add_ideas = MEX_UNIT_LOZ_PARA_FORCE
	add_ideas = MEX_UNIT_MAD_RED_SHIRT


	clear_array = MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array
	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array = token:MEX_UNIT_SOLDIER }
	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array = token:MEX_UNIT_DFS_AGENT }
	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array = token:MEX_UNIT_FJP }
	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array = token:MEX_UNIT_AIR_STRIKE }

	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_recruit_unit_button_array = 0 }

	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_govn_guerillas_found = token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT }

	## ENEMIES OF THE STATE

	set_variable = { FARMERS = 9 }
	set_variable = { FARMERS_POWER = 0.2 }
	set_variable = { FARMERS_NODE_DIST = 1 }
	set_variable = { FARMERS_HEALTH = 10 }
	set_variable = { FARMERS_TACTICS = 0.5 } #by virtue of knowing the terrain

	set_variable = { THUGS = 10 } #rightoid
	set_variable = { THUGS_POWER = 0.4 }
	set_variable = { THUGS_NODE_DIST = 1 }
	set_variable = { THUGS_HEALTH = 20 }
	set_variable = { THUGS_TACTICS = 0.2 }

	set_variable = { PARAMILITARY = 11 } #both
	set_variable = { PARAMILITARY_POWER = 0.6 }
	set_variable = { PARAMILITARY_NODE_DIST = 3 }
	set_variable = { PARAMILITARY_HEALTH = 60 }
	set_variable = { PARAMILITARY_TACTICS = 0.5 }


	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX_DW_zoom_array^num = 0 }
		}
		clear_array = MEX_DW_zoom_array
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_zoom_array = 1 }
	}

	clear_array = MEX_DW_placeholder
	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_placeholder = 1 }

	# Setup base node info

	set_temp_variable = { MEX_max_DW_node_number = 800 }

	clear_array = MEX_DW_locations
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 1
		end = MEX_max_DW_node_number
		value = j

		var:j = {
			MEX_DW_setup_node = yes
		}
	}

	# Setup node data
	MEX_build_DW_map = yes


	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 1
		end = MEX_max_DW_node_number
		value = j

		var:j = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { MEX_DW_x > 0 }
						check_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = 1 }
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { MEX.MEX_DW_locations = j }
				set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_next_location_id = j}
				add_to_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_next_location_id = 1 }

				set_variable = { MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT_control = 90 }
				set_variable = { MEX_Faction_THE_GPG_control = 10 }
				set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT}

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { MEX_DW_x > 0 }
				}
				add_to_array = { MEX.MEX_DW_locations = j }
				set_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_next_location_id = j}
				add_to_variable = { MEX.MEX_DW_next_location_id = 1 }
			}
		}
	}


	MEX_DW_refresh_control_pie_charts = yes

	set_variable = { MEX_main_stronghold = 4 }

	MEX_setup_DW_connections = yes

	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_locations
		value = nodestuff

		var:nodestuff = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { MEX_DW_node_type = 1 }
				}
				set_variable = { MEX_DW_intel = 100 }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = MEX_DW_connections
					value = nodeneighbour


					var:nodeneighbour = {
						set_temp_variable_to_random = {
							var = random_intel
							min = 10
							max = 50
							integer = yes
						}
						set_variable = { MEX_DW_intel = random_intel }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { MEX_DW_intel > 25 }
							}
							set_variable = { MEX_DW_controller = token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT }
						}
					}

				}
			}
		}
	}

	clear_array = MEX_DW_action_log_times
	clear_array = MEX_DW_action_log_actors
	clear_array = MEX_DW_action_log_types
	clear_array = MEX_DW_action_log_targets

	#left side gui setup
	add_to_array = { MEX_DW_more_info_box = 0 }
	set_variable = { active_leftist_guerrillas = 5 } #There is only 4 active leftist guerrillas currently at startup but I added 1 extra variable to make the frame work correctly, this will mean that there will always be 1 extra guerrilla in this variable
	set_variable = { active_rightist_guerrillas = 3 } #There is only 2 active rightist guerrillas currently at startup, did the same thing as above
	set_variable = { dw_intensity = 10 }

	MEX_DW_filter_actions_or_events = yes
}
MEX_DW_update_gui_elements = {
	MEX_DW_refresh_control_pie_charts = yes
	MEX_DW_update_intel_progbar = yes
	MEX_DW_find_if_more_than_one_unit_fac = yes
}
MEX_DW_update_intel_progbar = {
	set_variable = { MEX_DW_intel_animprog = MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_DW_intel }
	multiply_variable = { MEX_DW_intel_animprog = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { intel_progbar_anim_update = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { intel_progbar_anim_update = 2 }
		}
		set_variable = { intel_progbar_anim_update = 0 }
	}
}

MEX_DW_filter_actions_or_events = {
	clear_array = MEX_DW_action_log_times
	clear_array = MEX_DW_event_log_times

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX_DW_ev_ac_click = 0 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = MEX_DW_events
			value = event_value

			add_to_array = { MEX_DW_event_log_times = event_value }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX_DW_ev_ac_click = 1 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = MEX_DW_actions
			value = action_value

			add_to_array = { MEX_DW_action_log_times = action_value }
		}
	}
}

MEX_DW_refresh_control_pie_charts = {
	clear_array = MEX_DW_is_city
	clear_array = MEX_DW_is_town
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_DW_node_type = 1 }
		}
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_is_city = 1 }
		#govt
		set_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_govt_st = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_govt_end = MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT_control }

		set_variable = { control_frame@token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT = MEX_DW_govt_st }
		round_variable = control_frame@token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT
		multiply_variable = { control_frame@token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT = 1000 }
		add_to_variable = { control_frame@token:MEX_Faction_GOVERNMENT = MEX_DW_govt_end }

		set_temp_variable = { valueeeee = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_fac_st = MEX_DW_govt_end }
		set_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_fac_end = MEX_DW_fac_st }
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = { check_variable = { valueeeee < MEX_DW_ALL_GROUPS^num } }
			set_temp_variable = { fac = MEX_DW_ALL_GROUPS^valueeeee }


			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					add_to_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_fac_end = MEX_DW_selected_location:[GROUP_NAME]_control }
				}
				GROUP_NAME = "[?fac.GetTokenKey]"
			}
			set_variable = { control_frame@var:fac = MEX_DW_fac_st }
			round_variable = control_frame@var:fac
			multiply_variable = { control_frame@var:fac = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { control_frame@var:fac = MEX_DW_fac_end }

			set_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_fac_st = MEX_DW_fac_end }
			set_temp_variable = { MEX_DW_fac_end = MEX_DW_fac_st }

			add_to_temp_variable = { valueeeee = 1 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_DW_node_type = 0 }
				check_variable = { MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_DW_node_type = 2 }
			}

		}
		add_to_array = { MEX_DW_is_town = 1 }
		clear_array = Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location

		if = {
			limit = {
				var:MEX_DW_selected_location = {
					MEX_dw_is_node_allegence_known = yes
				}
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = MEX_DW_ALL_GROUPS
				value = group_value

				for_each_loop = {
					array = MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_DW_node_units
					value = unit_value
					break = break

					if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { unit_value:MEX_DW_alliegance = group_value }
								NOT = {
									is_in_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
						set_variable = { Reason_for_inf@var:group_value = 0 }

					}

				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_DW_controller = group_value }
							NOT = {
								is_in_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
					set_variable = { Reason_for_inf@var:group_value = 1 }
				}

				for_each_loop = {
					array = MEX_DW_selected_location:MEX_DW_connections
					value = connection_value
					break = break_2


					for_each_loop = {
						array = connection_value:MEX_DW_node_units
						value = unit_value
						break = break

						if = {
							limit = {
								AND = {
									check_variable = { unit_value:MEX_DW_alliegance = group_value }
									NOT = {
										is_in_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
									}
								}
							}
							add_to_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
							set_variable = { Reason_for_inf@var:group_value = 2 }
							log = [?group_value.GetTokenKey]
						}
					}

					if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { connection_value:MEX_DW_controller = group_value }
								NOT = {
									is_in_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = group_value }
						set_variable = { Reason_for_inf@var:group_value = 3 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Factions_Influencing^num@var:MEX_DW_selected_location > 3 }
				}
				add_to_array = { Factions_Influencing@var:MEX_DW_selected_location = 3 }
			}



		}

	}


}
Mex_heletetwt = {
	set_temp_variable = { node_To = 336 }
	MEX_DW_Should_Battle_Start = yes
}
MEX_DW_Should_Battle_Start = {

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { node_To:MEX_DW_node_units^num > 1 }
			check_variable = { node_To:MEX_DW_intel > 25 } #arb
		}

		set_temp_variable = { first_unit = node_To:MEX_DW_node_units^0 }
		set_temp_variable = { first_unit_alliegance = first_unit:MEX_DW_alliegance }
		log = [?first_unit_alliegance]

		for_each_loop = {
			array = node_To:MEX_DW_node_units
			value = checker_unit_val

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { checker_unit_val:MEX_DW_alliegance = first_unit_alliegance }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { node_To:Is_In_Battle = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

}
MEX_DW_find_if_more_than_one_unit_fac = {
	var:MEX_DW_selected_location = {
		clear_array = Node_Not_Battle
		clear_array = Node_In_Battle
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { MEX_DW_selected_location:Is_In_Battle = 0 }
		}
		var:MEX_DW_selected_location = {
			add_to_array = { Node_Not_Battle = 1 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		var:MEX_DW_selected_location = {
			add_to_array = { Node_In_Battle = 1 }
		}
	}
}

MEX_DW_euclidean_dist = {
	set_temp_variable = { xA = node_1:MEX_DW_x }
	set_temp_variable = { yA = node_1:MEX_DW_y }

	set_temp_variable = { xB = node_2:MEX_DW_x }
	set_temp_variable = { yB = node_2:MEX_DW_y }

	set_temp_variable = { xDiff = xB }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { xDiff = xA }

	set_temp_variable = { yDiff = yB }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { yDiff = yA }
	divide_temp_variable = { xDiff = 100 }
	divide_temp_variable = { yDiff = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { xDiff = xDiff }

	multiply_temp_variable = { yDiff = yDiff }

	set_temp_variable = { dist_sqrd = 0 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { dist_sqrd = xDiff }
	add_to_temp_variable = { dist_sqrd = yDiff }

	set_temp_variable = { eucdist = dist_sqrd}
}
MEX_DW_test = {
	set_temp_variable = { node_A = args^0 }
	set_temp_variable = { node_B = args^1 }

	MEX_dw_node_traversal = yes

}

MEX_dw_node_traversal = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = MEX_DW_locations
		value = loc

		set_variable = { loc:g_val = 1000 }
		set_variable = { loc:f_val = 0 }
	}

	clear_array = open_list
	clear_array = closed_list
	clear_array = path
	log = [?node_B]

	set_variable = { node_A:g_val = 0 }

	add_to_array = { open_list = node_A }

	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { open_list^num > 0 }
		}
		break = break

		clear_variable = current_node
		set_variable = { min = open_list^0 }

		for_each_loop = {
			array = open_list
			value = opennodes

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { opennodes:f_val < min:f_val }
				}
				set_variable = { min = opennodes }
			}
		}

		set_variable = { current_node = min }

		remove_from_array = { array = open_list		value = min }

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_node = node_B }
			}
			log = [?current_node]
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { current_node = node_A }
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { path = current_node }
				set_variable = { current_node = current_node:parent }
			}
			add_to_array = { path = current_node }
			set_temp_variable = { break = 1 }
		}

		add_to_array = { closed_list = current_node }

		for_each_loop = {
			array = current_node:MEX_DW_connections
			value = exploringnodes

			set_temp_variable = { node_1 = exploringnodes }
			set_temp_variable = { node_2 = node_A }
			MEX_DW_euclidean_dist = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tempg = eucdist }
			add_to_temp_variable = { tempg = current_node:g_val }

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { tempg < exploringnodes:g_val }
				}
				set_variable = { exploringnodes:parent = current_node }
				set_variable = { exploringnodes:g_val = tempg }
				add_to_variable = { exploringnodes:f_val = tempg }
				set_temp_variable = { node_1 = exploringnodes }
				set_temp_variable = { node_2 = node_B }
				MEX_DW_euclidean_dist = yes
				add_to_variable = { exploringnodes:f_val = eucdist }

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_in_array = {
								array = closed_list
								value = exploringnodes
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { open_list = exploringnodes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
